heading\n- **stackable/icon-label** | Icon Label (stk-type: special) | stk-required-blocks: icon, heading | Icon+text pair\n- **stackable/icon-list-item** | Icon List Item (stk-type: hidden) | parent: icon-list | usesContext: ordered, uniqueId\n- **stackable/image-box** | Image Box (stk-type: special) | stk-required-blocks: image, subtitle, icon | Hover effect block\n- **stackable/map** | Map (stk-type: special) | Google Maps embedded block\n- **stackable/notification** | Notification (stk-type: special) | providesContext: innerBlockOrientation | stk-required-blocks: icon | Alert/notice display\n- **stackable/number-box** | Number Box (stk-type: special) | Step/method display\n- **stackable/price** | Price (stk-type: special) | stk-required-blocks: text | Currency display with styling\n- **stackable/progress-bar** | Progress Bar (stk-type: special) | Percentage visualization\n- **stackable/progress-circle** | Progress Circle (stk-type: special) | Circular progress indicator\n- **stackable/separator** | Separator (stk-type: special) | SVG divider with shapes\n- **stackable/spacer** | Spacer (stk-type: special) | Vertical spacing\n- **stackable/subtitle** | Subtitle (stk-type: special) | Global typography styling\n- **stackable/table-of-contents** | Table of Contents (stk-type: special) | Auto-generated from headings\n- **stackable/timeline** | Timeline (stk-type: special) | Chronological event display\n- **stackable/video-popup** | Video Popup (stk-type: special) | stk-required-blocks: icon, image | Lightbox video embed\n\n#### Section Blocks (11 blocks)\n- **stackable/call-to-action** | Call to Action (stk-type: section) | providesContext: innerBlockOrientation | stk-substitution-blocks: heading, text, button-group, button\n- **stackable/feature** | Feature (stk-type: section) | providesContext: columnWrapDesktop | stk-required-blocks: image | Product feature showcase\n- **stackable/feature-grid** | Feature Grid (stk-type: section) | Multiple features display\n- **stackable/hero** | Hero (stk-type: section) | providesContext: innerBlockOrientation | stk-substitution-blocks: heading, text, button-group, button\n- **stackable/horizontal-scroller** | Horizontal Scroller (stk-type: special) | providesContext: columnFit | Horizontal slider\n- **stackable/icon-box** | Icon Box (stk-type: section) | Icon+text summary\n- **stackable/posts** | Posts (stk-type: special) | providesContext: type, orderBy, order, taxonomyType, taxonomy, numberOfItems | Blog query loop\n- **stackable/pricing-box** | Pricing Box (stk-type: section) | stk-required-blocks: price, text, icon-list | stk-substitution-blocks: heading, subtitle, button-group\n- **stackable/tabs** | Tabs (stk-type: special) | providesContext: initialTabOpen, tabOrientation, tabPanelEffect, equalTabHeight | Complex composition\n- **stackable/tab-labels** (stk-type: hidden) | parent: tabs | Navigation for tabs\n- **stackable/tab-content** (stk-type: hidden) | parent: tabs | Content container for tabs\n- **stackable/team-member** | Team Member (stk-type: section) | providesContext: innerBlockOrientation | stk-substitution-blocks: image, heading, subtitle, text, button\n- **stackable/testimonial** | Testimonial (stk-type: section) | providesContext: innerBlockOrientation | stk-required-blocks: image-box\n- **stackable/blockquote** | Blockquote (stk-type: section)\n\n#### Hidden/Special Blocks (3 blocks)\n- **stackable/column** | Inner Column (stk-type: hidden) | parent: columns, carousel, feature, feature-grid, horizontal-scroller, tab-content | usesContext: columnWrapDesktop | availableStates: enabled, hidden\n- **stackable/design-library** | Design Library (stk-type: special) | Template/pattern selector | availableStates: enabled, hidden\n\n#### File Locations (All in `/src/block/[block-name]/`):\n- Each block has `block.json` file with metadata\n- Block registration structure: `apiVersion: 3, name: stackable/[name], title, description, category: stackable, textdomain: stackable-ultimate-gutenberg-blocks`\n- Complex blocks have `index.php` for frontend script enqueuing (e.g., tabs block)\n\n---\n\n### 2. BLOCK PATTERNS & TEMPLATES\n\n**Design Library Architecture:**\n- **Location:** `/src/design-library/init.php`\n- **API Version:** v4\n- **Block:** `stackable/design-library` (stk-type: special)\n- **REST Routes:** \n  - `stackable/v2/design_library/{type}` - GET with permission check for `edit_posts`\n  - `stackable/v3/design_library_image` - POST for image download\n- **Features:**\n  - Cloud-based design library integration\n  - Hundreds of ready-made designs and page templates\n  - Pattern library with block layouts\n  - Transient caching system (delete via `stackable_delete_design_library_cache` action)\n  - Design inheritance from Block Themes\n  - Multiple shape separator designs\n\n**Pattern System:**\n- Uses REST API for pattern delivery\n- Designs inherit theme.json styles\n- Pattern library provides pre-built page layouts\n- No traditional `register_block_pattern()` calls found - patterns sourced from cloud API\n\n---\n\n### 3. SHARED ARCHITECTURE\n\n#### 3a. Global Design Tokens (`create_global_schema()`)\n**File:** `/src/global-settings.php` (lines 102-126)\n\nThe `create_global_schema()` static function creates responsive schemas with device-specific and hover-state variants:\n\n```\nSchema Structure:\n├─ desktop: <type>\n├─ tablet: <type>\n├─ mobile: <type>\n├─ desktopHover: <type>\n├─ tabletHover: <type>\n├─ mobileHover: <type>\n├─ desktopParentHover: <type>\n├─ tabletParentHover: <type>\n├─ mobileParentHover: <type>\n├─ desktopUnit: string\n├─ tabletUnit: string\n├─ mobileUnit: string\n├─ desktopHoverUnit: string\n├─ tabletHoverUnit: string\n├─ mobileHoverUnit: string\n├─ desktopParentHoverUnit: string\n├─ tabletParentHoverUnit: string\n└─ mobileParentHoverUnit: string\n```\n\n**Helper Methods:**\n- `get_four_range_properties()` - Padding/margin objects with top, right, bottom, left\n- `get_string_four_range_properties()` - String-based four-range (colors, etc.)\n- `get_string_properties()` - Simple string type with device/hover variants\n- `get_number_properties()` - Numeric type with device/hover variants\n\n**Global Settings Registration:**\n- `stackable_global_colors` - Color palette (schema: name, slug, color, rgb)\n- `stackable_global_typography` - Font family, size, weight, line-height, letter-spacing (responsive + hover)\n- `stackable_global_typography_apply_to` - Setting scope (blocks-stackable, blocks-stackable-native, blocks-all)\n- `stackable_global_force_typography` - Force !important flag\n- `stackable_global_hide_theme_colors` - Color picker visibility\n- `stackable_global_hide_default_colors` - Color picker visibility\n- `stackable_global_hide_site_editor_colors` - Color picker visibility\n\n#### 3b. Dynamic Breakpoints (`/src/dynamic-breakpoints.php`)\n\n**Default Breakpoints:**\n- Desktop: 1024px (default)\n- Tablet: 768px (default) - Mobile starts here\n- Mobile: Below 768px\n\n**Custom Breakpoints:**\n- Saved in `stackable_dynamic_breakpoints` option\n- Applied via `adjust_breakpoints()` filter on all frontend CSS\n- Media query order (priority-based to prevent cascading issues):\n  ```\n  @media screen and (min-width:1024px) - Desktop only\n  @media screen and (min-width:768px) - Desktop & tablet\n  @media screen and (min-width:768px) and (max-width:1023px) - Tablet only\n  @media screen and (max-width:1023px) - Tablet & mobile\n  @media screen and (max-width:767px) - Mobile only\n  ```\n- **CLS Prevention:** Responsive CSS loaded via `load_frontend_scripts_conditionally_head()` to prevent layout shift\n- Shortcut media queries replaced before breakpoint adjustment\n\n#### 3c. CSS Optimization (`/src/css-optimize.php`)\n\n**System:** Stackable_CSS_Optimize class\n\n**Process:**\n1. When post is saved, generates optimized CSS for all blocks (pre-calculated)\n2. Caches optimized CSS in post meta (loaded in frontend head)\n3. Original block styles stripped in `render_block` filter\n4. Backward compatible - falls back to original rendering if no optimization\n\n**Benefits:**\n- No CSS processing during page load\n- Compatible with caching plugins\n- Post content/blocks unchanged\n- Optimized for Core Web Vitals\n\n**Media Query Order:**\n```\nLine 64-71:\n'' (All screens)\n'@media screen and (min-width:1024px)' - Desktop\n'@media screen and (min-width:768px)' - Desktop & tablet\n'@media screen and (min-width:768px) and (max-width:1023px)' - Tablet\n'@media screen and (max-width:1023px)' - Tablet & mobile\n'@media screen and (max-width:767px)' - Mobile\n```\n\n---\n\n### 4. CSS ARCHITECTURE\n\n#### 4a. Asset Loading (`/src/init.php`)\n\n**Frontend Stylesheet Stack:**\n```\nLine 97-102:\n- ugb-style-css (frontend_blocks.css)\n- Dependencies: filters via stackable_frontend_css_dependencies\n- Version: STACKABLE_VERSION (3.19.7)\n\nLine 113-119:\n- ugb-style-css-responsive (frontend_blocks_responsive.css)\n- Depends on: ugb-style-css\n- Enqueued always for responsive design\n\nLine 127-131:\n- ugb-style-css-nodep (no dependencies)\n- Inline styles via stackable_inline_styles_nodep filter\n- Global styles loaded without cascading\n\nLine 134-138:\n- ugb-block-style-inheritance-nodep\n- Theme.json block style inheritance\n- From filter: stackable_block_style_inheritance_inline_styles_nodep\n```\n\n**Frontend JavaScript:**\n- Conditional loading via `load_frontend_scripts_conditionally()` (line 44)\n- Early detection in `load_frontend_scripts_conditionally_head()` (line 45)\n- Only loads when Stackable block detected in post content\n- Performance check: searches for `<!-- wp:stackable/` marker\n\n**Editor Assets:**\n- `enqueue_block_editor_assets` - Editor scripts/styles\n- `enqueue_block_assets` - Editor iframe head styles (priority 50)\n- `register_block_editor_assets()` - All editor-only assets\n\n#### 4b. Frontend CSS Structure\n\n**File:** `/dist/frontend_blocks.css`\n\n**Block Styling:**\n- `.stk-block` class prefix for all blocks\n- `.stk-block-[name]` for specific blocks\n- Per-instance CSS via inline styles (optimized & cached)\n- CSS variables for reactive design updates\n\n**Responsive CSS:** `/dist/frontend_blocks_responsive.css`\n\nContains all responsive rules for:\n- Column layout calculations (flex: 50%, 33.33%, 25%, 20%, 16.66%, etc.)\n- Tab layouts (vertical vs horizontal with CSS grid)\n- Alignment utilities (center, left, right, space-between, space-around)\n- Mobile-specific layouts (flex-direction: column-reverse for features)\n- Hide/show utilities (.stk--hide-desktop, .stk--hide-tablet, .stk--hide-mobile)\n- Separator styles with alignment\n- Timeline mobile polyfill (CSS grid layout)\n- Button group collapse behaviors\n\n#### 4c. Per-Block CSS Implementation\n\n**CSS Variables Pattern:**\n- Desktop: `--stk-property`\n- Tablet: `--stk-property` (overridden)\n- Mobile: `--stk-property` (overridden)\n- Hover states: JavaScript class toggling\n- Custom data attributes via `data-*` on elements\n\n**Example (Divider Block):**\n```css\n.stk-block-divider {\n  --stk-dots-margin-left: 0;\n  --stk-dots-margin-right: auto;\n}\n@media (center-aligned) {\n  --stk-dots-margin-right: auto;\n  --stk-dots-margin-left: auto;\n}\n```\n\n#### 4d. CLS Prevention Strategies\n\n1. **Head-based CSS Loading** - Load optimized CSS in `<head>` before DOM renders\n2. **Inline Styles Optimization** - Pre-calculated during post save\n3. **Container Queries** - Support for CSS containment (modern browsers)\n4. **Block Width Defaults** - Added via `add_block_widths()` action (line 65-66)\n5. **Responsive Image Loading** - Optimized for mobile speeds\n6. **CSS-in-JS Minimization** - Zero block-level JavaScript-generated styles on initial render\n\n---\n\n### 5. BLOCK COMPOSITION PATTERN\n\n#### 5a. InnerBlocks System\n\n**Parent-Child Relationships (block.json):**\n\nComplex blocks using InnerBlocks:\n- **stackable/columns** ← Contains → stackable/column (multiple, restricted parent)\n- **stackable/tabs** ← Contains → stackable/tab-labels + stackable/tab-content\n- **stackable/tab-content** ← Contains → stackable/column (flexible)\n- **stackable/carousel** ← Contains → stackable/column (flexible)\n- **stackable/horizontal-scroller** ← Contains → stackable/column (flexible)\n- **stackable/button-group** ← Contains → stackable/button | stackable/icon-button (variants)\n- **stackable/icon-list** ← Contains → stackable/icon-list-item (restricted)\n- **stackable/feature** ← Contains → stackable/column (flexible)\n- **stackable/feature-grid** ← Contains → stackable/column (flexible)\n\n**Block Properties Defining Composition:**\n- `\"parent\": [\"parent-block\"]` - Restricts where block can be placed\n- `\"providesContext\": { \"contextKey\": \"propertyName\" }` - Passes data to children\n- `\"usesContext\": [\"contextKey\"]` - Consumes parent context\n- `\"stk-required-blocks\": []` - Required child blocks (substitutable)\n- `\"stk-substitution-blocks\": []` - Blocks that can replace required ones\n\n#### 5b. Context System (Responsive & State)\n\n**Context Providers (providesContext in block.json):**\n\n1. **stackable/innerBlockOrientation**\n   - Providers: columns, call-to-action, card, feature, hero, notification, pricing-box, team-member, testimonial\n   - Value: `innerBlockOrientation` property from block attributes\n   - Purpose: Tell children the parent's layout orientation\n\n2. **stackable/columnWrapDesktop**\n   - Providers: columns, feature, feature-grid\n   - Value: `columnWrapDesktop` property\n   - Purpose: Control column wrapping behavior at breakpoints\n\n3. **stackable/columnFit**\n   - Provider: horizontal-scroller\n   - Value: `columnFit` property\n   - Purpose: Control scrollable item sizing\n\n4. **stackable/initialTabOpen**\n   - Provider: tabs\n   - Value: `initialTabOpen` property\n   - Purpose: Set initially open tab index\n\n5. **stackable/tabOrientation**\n   - Provider: tabs\n   - Value: `tabOrientation` property (horizontal/vertical)\n   - Purpose: Tab layout direction\n\n6. **stackable/tabPanelEffect**\n   - Provider: tabs\n   - Value: `tabPanelEffect` property (fade, slide, none)\n   - Purpose: Tab content transition animation\n\n7. **stackable/equalTabHeight**\n   - Provider: tabs\n   - Value: `equalTabHeight` property\n   - Purpose: Force equal height tab panels\n\n8. **stackable/ordered**\n   - Provider: icon-list\n   - Value: `ordered` property (boolean)\n   - Purpose: Ordered vs unordered list\n\n9. **stackable/uniqueId**\n   - Provider: icon-list\n   - Value: `uniqueId` property\n   - Purpose: Unique identifier for list items\n\n10. **Posts Query Context** (from stackable/posts)\n    - type, orderBy, order, taxonomyType, taxonomy, taxonomyFilterType\n    - postOffset, postExclude, postInclude, numberOfItems, stkQueryId\n\n#### 5c. Block Type Classification\n\n**Stackable Type System** (`stk-type` in block.json):\n- `essential` - Core building blocks (columns, heading, text, image, etc.)\n- `special` - Feature-rich individual blocks (accordion, carousel, tabs, etc.)\n- `section` - Full-width content sections (hero, feature, pricing, testimonial)\n- `hidden` - Internal blocks requiring parent (button, column, tab-labels, tab-content, icon-list-item)\n\n**Block Dependencies** (`stk-block-dependency`):\n- Format: \"parent-block|variant-name\"\n- Example: \"stackable/button-group|button\" - Button depends on button-group container\n- Ensures blocks load dependency chains correctly\n\n#### 5d. Composition Example: Tabs Block\n\n**File:** `/src/block/tabs/block.json` (lines 1-20)\n\n```json\nStructure:\nstackable/tabs (parent)\n├─ providesContext: initialTabOpen, tabOrientation, tabPanelEffect, equalTabHeight\n├─ Contains (flex layout):\n│  ├─ stackable/tab-labels (first child, navigation)\n│  │  ├─ usesContext: initialTabOpen, tabOrientation\n│  │  └─ Contains: stackable/tab-label items (implicit structure)\n│  └─ stackable/tab-content (flex layout, grid on mobile)\n│     ├─ usesContext: tabPanelEffect, equalTabHeight\n│     └─ Contains: stackable/column items (flexible)\n```\n\n**CSS Rendering:**\n```css\nDesktop (1024px+):\n.stk-block-tabs > .stk-inner-blocks {\n  grid-template-columns: auto 1fr auto; /* vertical layout */\n}\n\nMobile (<768px):\n.stk-block-tabs > .stk-inner-blocks {\n  grid-template-columns: 1fr; /* stacked layout */\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n### 6. ADVANCED FEATURES\n\n#### 6a. Hover State System\n\n**Architecture:** Device-specific hover states via CSS classes + CSS variables\n\n**Hover State Schema (lines 109-123 in global-settings.php):**\n```\nPer property:\n- desktopHover: Hover state on desktop\n- tabletHover: Hover state on tablet\n- mobileHover: Hover state on mobile\n- desktopParentHover: Hover state when parent is hovered\n- tabletParentHover: Hover state when parent is hovered\n- mobileParentHover: Hover state when parent is hovered\n- [*]HoverUnit: Unit for hover value (px, %, etc.)\n```\n\n**Implementation (color-schemes/index.php):**\n- Line 449: `'desktopHover' => '-hover'` - CSS class suffix\n- Lines 474-601: Hover color inheritance logic\n- Line 580: State-based suffix generation (`$suffix = $state === 'desktopHover' ? '-hover' : ''`)\n- Lines 625-627: Button plain style hover defaults\n- Line 668: Merging desktop + desktopHover declarations into single CSS rule\n\n**Color Scheme Hover States:**\n- Button hover colors auto-generate from outline colors\n- Icon hover colors inherit from background hover states\n- Parent hover cascades to children (parentHover states)\n\n#### 6b. Transform & Transition Controls\n\n**Global Controls Available:**\n- Transform: translate, scale, rotate, skew\n- Transition: duration, timing-function, delay\n- Filter effects: blur, brightness, contrast, grayscale, hue-rotate, invert, opacity, saturate, sepia\n- Animation states: hover, parent-hover (from global-settings registration)\n\n**Implementation via:**\n- CSS variables for values\n- Class-based hover triggers\n- Responsive device-specific variants\n\n#### 6c. Content Alignment System\n\n**Alignment Utilities:**\nClasses in responsive CSS (dynamic-breakpoints.php, lines 15-19):\n```\n.has-text-align-center\n.has-text-align-left\n.has-text-align-right\n.has-text-align-justify\n.has-text-align-space-between\n.has-text-align-space-around\n.has-text-align-space-evenly\n```\n\n**CSS Variables Generated:**\n```\n--stk-alignment-margin-left\n--stk-alignment-margin-right\n--stk-alignment-padding-left\n--stk-alignment-justify-content\n--stk-alignment-text-align\n```\n\n**Responsive Variants:**\n- `-tablet` suffix for tablet-specific alignment\n- `-mobile` suffix for mobile-specific alignment\n- Layout adjusts via flexbox justify-content property\n\n#### 6d. Dynamic Content Integration\n\n**Posts Block (stackable/posts):**\n- Query parameters via context: type, orderBy, order, taxonomyType, taxonomy\n- Post offset, include, exclude lists\n- Dynamic query ID (stkQueryId)\n- Integrates with native WordPress Query Loop API\n\n**Meta Field Support:**\n- All blocks support `data-*` attributes for custom data\n- Template engine hook system for rendering customization\n\n#### 6e. Global Typography System\n\n**Schema (lines 295-349 in global-settings.php):**\n```\nFont Properties:\n- fontFamily: string\n- fontSize: number (device variants: tablet, mobile)\n- fontSizeUnit: string (px, em, rem, %)\n- fontWeight: string (300, 400, 600, bold, etc.)\n- textTransform: string (none, uppercase, lowercase, capitalize)\n- lineHeight: number (device variants)\n- lineHeightUnit: string\n- letterSpacing: number (device variants)\n- letterSpacingUnit: string\n```\n\n**Application Methods (global-settings.php):**\n- Line 60: `color_add_global_styles` filter - Frontend color styles\n- Line 82: `typography_detect_native_blocks` - Apply to native blocks\n- Line 89: `typography_add_global_styles` filter - Frontend typography styles\n- Line 76: `typography_parse_global_styles` - Parse global settings on `after_setup_theme`\n\n**Typography Detection:**\n- Detects which global typography settings are used\n- Applies only when enabled (checks `apply_typography_to` option)\n- Supports forcing !important flag via `stackable_global_force_typography`\n\n**Scope Options (line 273-280):**\n- `blocks-stackable` - Stackable blocks only\n- `blocks-stackable-native` - Stackable + WordPress native blocks\n- `blocks-all` - All block types\n\n---\n\n### 7. PLUGIN ARCHITECTURE\n\n#### 7a. Initialization Flow (`/src/init.php`)\n\n1. **Asset Registration** (register_frontend_assets, lines 95-130)\n   - `ugb-style-css` - Frontend styles\n   - `ugb-style-css-responsive` - Responsive styles\n   - `ugb-style-css-nodep` - No-dependency inline styles\n   - `ugb-block-style-inheritance-nodep` - Theme.json inheritance\n\n2. **Conditional Loading** (load_frontend_scripts_conditionally, line 44)\n   - Checks for Stackable blocks during render_block filter\n   - Loads CSS/JS only when needed\n   - CLS-prevention via head loader (line 45)\n\n3. **Editor Integration** (enqueue_block_editor_assets, lines 39-52)\n   - Editor scripts: `ugb-block-js`\n   - Editor styles: `ugb-block-editor-css`\n   - Translation strings via `stackable_load_js_translations()`\n\n4. **Theme Compatibility** (add_body_class_theme_compatibility, line 68)\n   - Detects theme and adds compatibility classes\n   - Applies to both frontend and admin body\n\n#### 7b. Block Registration System (`/src/blocks.php`)\n\n**Process (lines 17-42):**\n1. Gets blocks array via `stackable.blocks` filter\n2. Unregisters existing versions (for updates)\n3. Applies `stackable.register-blocks.options` filter\n4. Sets default register options:\n   - `'style': 'ugb-style-css'`\n   - `'editor_script': 'ugb-block-js'`\n   - `'editor_style': 'ugb-block-editor-css'`\n5. Merges metadata with options\n6. Registers via `register_block_type()`\n\n**Block Array Sources:**\n- Loaded from `stackable_get_blocks_array()` function in `/src/stk-block-types.php`\n- Generated file listing all 46 blocks with full metadata\n- Includes stk-type, stk-demo URLs, required/substitution blocks\n\n#### 7c. Global Settings System\n\n**Classes/Files:**\n- `Stackable_Global_Settings` - Global colors, typography (global-settings.php)\n- `Stackable_Editor_Settings` - Editor UI settings (editor-settings.php)\n- Plugin system via `/src/plugins/` directory\n\n**Editor Settings Registered (editor-settings.php):**\n- `stackable_hide_cimo_notice` - Hide download notice\n- `stackable_block_states` - Block visibility/enable states per user\n- `stackable_google_maps_api_key` - Maps block API key\n- `stackable_enable_design_library` - Design library visibility toggle\n- `stackable_optimize_inline_css` - CSS optimization feature flag\n\n#### 7d. Plugin System\n\n**Modules in `/src/plugins/`:**\n- `global-settings/` - Global design tokens and color schemes\n  - `preset-controls/` - Preset management UI\n  - `color-schemes/` - Color palette management (includes hover logic)\n  - `spacing-and-borders/` - Global spacing controls\n  - `buttons-and-icons/` - Global button/icon styling\n  - `block-styles/` - Block style inheritance from theme\n- `theme-block-style-inheritance/` - Integration with theme.json\n\n#### 7e. Feature Flags & Compatibility\n\n**Pro vs Free:**\n- `STACKABLE_BUILD` constant (free/pro)\n- `STACKABLE_SHOW_PRO_NOTICES` - Pro feature announcements\n- Freemius SDK integration for upsells\n\n**Compatibility Layers:**\n- `/src/compatibility/woocommerce.php` - WooCommerce integration\n- `/src/compatibility/ewww.php` - EWWW image optimization\n- `/src/compatibility/blocksy/` - Blocksy theme compatibility\n- `/src/compatibility/neve/` - Neve theme compatibility\n\n---\n\n### 8. KEY PERFORMANCE FEATURES\n\n**File Size:**\n- Frontend CSS + JS: ~7.8kb total (gzipped)\n- Zero jQuery dependencies\n- No bloatware\n\n**Optimization Techniques:**\n1. CSS pre-calculation on post save (CSS_Optimize class)\n2. Conditional script loading (detects Stackable blocks)\n3. Responsive CSS in separate file\n4. Inline style deduplication\n5. Media query ordering to prevent cascading\n\n**Core Web Vitals Support:**\n- LCP: Early CSS loading in `<head>` via `load_frontend_scripts_conditionally_head()`\n- FID: Minimal JavaScript\n- CLS: CSS variables prevent layout shifts, block widths pre-set\n\n---\n\n### 9. BLOCK PATTERNS & TEMPLATES\n\n**Pattern System:**\n- Design Library block provides cloud-based pattern/template system\n- No static `register_block_pattern` in WordPress Registry\n- Dynamic loading from CDN: `https://stackable-files.pages.dev`\n- API Version: v4\n- File: `/src/design-library/init.php`\n- REST Routes: `/stackable/v2/design_library/[type]`, `/stackable/v3/design_library_image`\n- Cache mechanism: transient-based (`stackable_get_design_library_json_v4`)\n- Includes:\n  - Hundreds of ready-made designs\n  - Dozens of full page templates\n  - Dozens of block layouts\n  - Shape separator designs\n  - Theme-aware design inheritance (theme.json support)\n\n---\n\n### 3. SHARED ARCHITECTURE\n\n#### Global Settings System\n**File:** `/src/global-settings.php` (Class: `Stackable_Global_Settings`)\n- **Global Design Tokens:**\n  - Global Color Palette (registered as `stackable_global_colors`)\n  - Global Typography Settings (heading, body text)\n  - Global Spacing & Borders\n  - Global Buttons & Icons\n  - Global Block Styles\n  - Color Schemes with inheritance\n  \n- **Schema Creation:** `create_global_schema()` method (line 102)\n  - Generates responsive device-based schema: desktop, tablet, mobile\n  - Supports hover states: desktopHover, tabletHover, mobileHover\n  - Supports parent hover: desktopParentHover, tabletParentHover, mobileParentHover\n  - Unit properties for each device and hover state\n  \n- **Global Typography Properties:**\n  - fontFamily, fontSize, fontWeight, textTransform\n  - lineHeight, letterSpacing\n  - Responsive variants for tablet/mobile\n  - Hover variants for interactive elements\n  \n- **Helper Methods:**\n  - `get_four_range_properties()` - Four-range schema (top, right, bottom, left)\n  - `get_string_four_range_properties()` - String variant\n  - `get_string_properties()` - String type schema\n  - `get_number_properties()` - Number type schema\n\n#### Dynamic Breakpoints System\n**File:** `/src/dynamic-breakpoints.php` (Class: `Stackable_Dynamic_Breakpoints`)\n- **Default Breakpoints:**\n  - Tablet: 1024px\n  - Mobile: 768px\n- **Custom User Breakpoints:** Stored in `stackable_dynamic_breakpoints` option\n- **Media Query Order (CLS prevention):**\n  - All screens\n  - Desktop only: min-width 1024px\n  - Desktop & tablet: min-width 768px\n  - Tablet only: 768px - 1023px\n  - Tablet & mobile: max-width 1023px\n  - Mobile: max-width 767px\n- **Frontend Adjustments:**\n  - Filter hook: `stackable_frontend_css` (adjusts all CSS)\n  - Filter hook: `render_block` (adjusts individual block styles)\n  - Enqueues responsive CSS conditionally\n  - Hook: `stackable_responsive_breakpoints` - allows custom breakpoints\n\n#### CSS Optimization System\n**File:** `/src/css-optimize.php` (Class: `Stackable_CSS_Optimize`)\n- **Optimization Process:**\n  - On post save: generates optimized CSS, caches in post meta\n  - Saves both optimized AND raw CSS values for verification\n  - Pre-calculates all CSS to avoid frontend processing\n  - Backward compatible with unoptimized blocks\n  \n- **Media Query Order (prevents wrong cascades):**\n  - `''` - All screens\n  - `@media screen and (min-width:1024px)` - Desktop\n  - `@media screen and (min-width:768px)` - Desktop & tablet\n  - `@media screen and (min-width:768px) and (max-width:1023px)` - Tablet only\n  - `@media screen and (max-width:1023px)` - Tablet & mobile\n  - `@media screen and (max-width:767px)` - Mobile\n\n- **Features:**\n  - Option: `stackable_optimize_inline_css` enables/disables optimization\n  - Strips optimized CSS from block rendering to avoid duplication\n  - CLS-aware: optimized CSS loads in head, prevents layout shift\n  - Works with caching plugins\n  - Protected meta: optimization data hidden from editor UI\n\n---\n\n### 4. CSS ARCHITECTURE\n\n#### Frontend Assets Loading\n**File:** `/src/init.php` (Class: `Stackable_Init`)\n\n**Main Stylesheets:**\n1. `ugb-style-css` - Frontend block styles\n   - Source: `dist/frontend_blocks.css`\n   - File: `/Users/varundubey/Local Sites/mediaverse/app/public/wp-content/plugins/stackable-ultimate-gutenberg-blocks/dist/frontend_blocks.css`\n   \n2. `ugb-style-css-responsive` - Responsive CSS\n   - Source: `dist/frontend_blocks_responsive.css`\n   - File: `/Users/varundubey/Local Sites/mediaverse/app/public/wp-content/plugins/stackable-ultimate-gutenberg-blocks/dist/frontend_blocks_responsive.css`\n   - Dependency: ugb-style-css\n\n3. `ugb-style-css-nodep` - Inline styles (no dependencies)\n   - Applied via filter: `stackable_inline_styles_nodep`\n   - Global colors, typography, global settings\n\n4. `ugb-block-style-inheritance-nodep` - Theme.json style inheritance\n   - Filter: `stackable_block_style_inheritance_inline_styles_nodep`\n\n**Editor Stylesheets:**\n- `ugb-block-editor-css` - Editor-specific styles\n- Source: `dist/editor_blocks.css`\n\n**Conditional Loading:**\n- Frontend: Checks post content for `<!-- wp:stackable/` comment blocks\n- Head loading: `load_frontend_scripts_conditionally_head()` - loads in `template_redirect` to prevent CLS\n- Fallback: Force loading available via `stackable_force_css_load` filter\n\n**Frontend Styles Structure:**\n- Block-level CSS: Per-instance styles inline\n- Global CSS: Color schemes, typography, spacing via filters\n- CSS Custom Properties (CSS Variables): Heavy use of --stk-* variables\n- Namespace: `.stk-block` class on all blocks\n\n#### Block-Level CSS (Per Instance)\n**Rendering:** Inline `<style>` tags within block HTML\n- Device-specific CSS variables\n- Hover state styles\n- Animation/transition values\n- Custom user overrides\n\n**CSS Custom Properties Used:**\n- `--stk-block-default-width` - Default block width\n- `--stk-block-width-default-detected` - Theme-detected width\n- `--stk-block-wide-width` - Wide alignment width\n- `--stk-column-gap` - Gap between columns\n- `--stk-alignment-*` - Text alignment CSS vars\n- `--stk-button-*` - Button styling vars\n- `--stk-*-hover` - Hover state properties\n\n#### CLS (Cumulative Layout Shift) Prevention\n\n**Strategies:**\n1. **Head CSS Loading:**\n   - Responsive CSS loads in `<head>` before content renders\n   - Function: `load_frontend_scripts_conditionally_head()` (line 172)\n   - Executes on `template_redirect` hook\n\n2. **Responsive Grid Sizing:**\n   - Column widths pre-calculated with CSS math\n   - Example: `flex: 1 1 calc(50% - var(--stk-column-gap, 0px)*1/2)`\n   - Prevents width recalculation when gap changes\n\n3. **Reserved Space:**\n   - Root variables for block margins, padding, container padding\n   - Applied before content renders\n   - Variables: `--stk-block-margin-bottom`, `--stk-container-padding`, etc.\n\n4. **Separator Height Handling:**\n   - Separator block has fixed height calculation\n   - Prevents top/bottom padding reflow\n   - Special mobile handling for separators\n\n---\n\n### 5. BLOCK COMPOSITION PATTERN\n\n#### InnerBlocks Architecture\n\n**Three Composition Types:**\n\n1. **Parent-Child Structure (Required Parent)**\n   - Examples: button → button-group, column → columns\n   - Parent specifies allowed children via `parent` key\n   - Child blocks check parent via parent key in block.json\n\n2. **Composition with stk-required-blocks**\n   - Parent block can enforce required child blocks\n   - Example: accordion requires icon-label, heading, icon\n   - File: block.json metadata key `stk-required-blocks`\n   - Allows flexible nesting but suggests block recommendations\n\n3. **Composition with stk-substitution-blocks**\n   - Blocks that can be replaced/edited within parent\n   - Example: call-to-action can substitute heading, text, button-group\n   - Allows users to add/replace without changing parent structure\n\n#### Context API Usage\n\n**providesContext Keys (Parent blocks publish these):**\n- `stackable/innerBlockOrientation` - Direction for child layout\n- `stackable/columnWrapDesktop` - Column wrap behavior on desktop\n- `stackable/columnFit` - Column fitting mode\n- `stackable/tabOrientation` - Horizontal vs vertical tabs\n- `stackable/initialTabOpen` - Which tab opens initially\n- `stackable/tabPanelEffect` - Tab transition effect\n- `stackable/equalTabHeight` - Equal tab heights\n- `stackable/ordered` - Ordered/unordered list type\n- `stackable/uniqueId` - Unique identifier for list items\n- Dynamic content context from Posts block: type, orderBy, order, taxonomy, postOffset, numberOfItems, stkQueryId\n\n**usesContext Keys (Child blocks consume):**\n- All children consume: `postId`, `postType`, `queryId`, `stackable/innerBlockOrientation`\n- Specialized consumers read appropriate context from parents\n\n#### Complex Composition Examples\n\n**Tabs Block Nesting:**\n```\ntabs (providesContext: initialTabOpen, tabOrientation, tabPanelEffect, equalTabHeight)\n├── tab-labels (parent: tabs, usesContext: tabOrientation, initialTabOpen)\n└── tab-content (parent: tabs, usesContext: tabPanelEffect, equalTabHeight)\n    └── column* (InnerBlocks allowed)\n```\n\n**Pricing Box Nesting:**\n```\npricing-box (stk-required-blocks: price, text, icon-list)\n├── price (required)\n├── text* (optional, substitution)\n├── icon-list (required)\n│   └── icon-list-item* (parent: icon-list)\n├── heading* (substitution)\n├── subtitle* (substitution)\n└── button-group* (substitution)\n    └── button* (parent: button-group)\n```\n\n**Feature Block Nesting:**\n```\nfeature (stk-required-blocks: image)\n├── image (required)\n├── heading* (substitution)\n├── text* (substitution)\n└── button-group* (substitution)\n    └── button* (parent: button-group)\n```\n\n---\n\n### 6. ADVANCED FEATURES\n\n#### Hover State System\n\n**Architecture:** Device + Hover State Combinations\n- Properties: `desktop`, `tablet`, `mobile`, `desktopHover`, `tabletHover`, `mobileHover`, `desktopParentHover`, `tabletParentHover`, `mobileParentHover`\n- Each state can have its own value\n- Units specified per device: `desktopUnit`, `tabletUnit`, `mobileUnit`, `desktopHoverUnit`, etc.\n\n**Rendering:**\n- Global hover styles: `/src/plugins/global-settings/color-schemes/index.php`\n- Suffix applied for hover: `-hover` class\n- Line 449: `'desktopHover' => '-hover'`\n- Parent hover inheritance: lines 474, 596-601\n- Color scheme hover values auto-applied when not specified (line 596)\n\n**Example Usage:**\n- Button color: desktop value\n- Button hover: desktopHover value\n- Button hover color fallback: can inherit from parent hover if not set\n\n#### Transform & Transition Controls\n\n**Storage:** Block attributes\n- Transform properties (rotate, scale, skew) stored per device\n- Transition timing stored per block\n- Render as inline CSS custom properties\n\n**Implementation:**\n- CSS variables passed to blocks\n- Applied via `transform:` CSS property\n- Transition values apply on all interactive elements\n- Mobile-specific disable: some transitions disabled on mobile\n\n#### Content Alignment System\n\n**Flexbox-based Architecture:**\n- All containers use flexbox\n- Alignment classes: `.has-text-align-center`, `.has-text-align-left`, `.has-text-align-right`\n- Responsive variants: `.has-text-align-center-tablet`, `.has-text-align-center-mobile`\n- Justify-content values via CSS variables: `--stk-alignment-justify-content`\n- Text-align values: `--stk-alignment-text-align`\n- Margin values for alignment: `--stk-alignment-margin-left`, `--stk-alignment-margin-right`\n\n**Example:** Call-to-action can be left/center/right aligned with responsive overrides\n\n#### Dynamic Content Integration\n\n**Posts Block (stackable/posts):**\n- Query Loop functionality\n- Provides context for dynamic post data\n- Context keys: type, orderBy, order, taxonomyType, taxonomy, taxonomyFilterType, postOffset, postExclude, postInclude, numberOfItems, stkQueryId\n- Can query different post types, taxonomies\n- Supports custom offsets and exclusions\n\n**Global Typography System:**\n- Applied to all Stackable blocks\n- Also applies to native WordPress blocks (optional)\n- Settings: `stackable_global_typography` option\n- Filter: `stackable_global_typography_selectors` to customize which elements receive global typography\n- Force important: `stackable_global_force_typography` option\n\n#### Global Typography System\n\n**Implementation:** `/src/global-settings.php`\n\n**Supported Properties:**\n- fontFamily\n- fontSize (desktop, tablet, mobile)\n- fontWeight\n- textTransform\n- lineHeight (desktop, tablet, mobile)\n- letterSpacing (desktop, tablet, mobile)\n- Font size unit variants\n\n**Application:**\n- Registers as `stackable_global_typography` setting (line 295+)\n- Frontend filter: `stackable_inline_styles_nodep` (line 89)\n- Method: `typography_add_global_styles()`\n- Can apply to:\n  - Stackable blocks only\n  - Stackable + native blocks\n  - All blocks\n- Controlled by: `stackable_global_typography_apply_to` option\n\n**Native 7. DESIGN SYSTEM FEATURES\n\n#### Global Settings Plugins\n**Directory:** `/src/plugins/global-settings/`\n\n**Components:**\n1. **Color Schemes** (`color-schemes/index.php`)\n   - Multiple color scheme support\n   - Light/dark mode variants\n   - Auto-hover generation\n   - Parent hover inheritance\n   - CSS variable generation\n   - Output: CSS custom properties with fallbacks\n\n2. **Spacing & Borders** (`spacing-and-borders/index.php`)\n   - Global spacing presets\n   - Border radius scales\n   - Border width presets\n   - Applied to all spacing controls\n\n3. **Buttons & Icons** (`buttons-and-icons/index.php`)\n   - Global button styles\n   - Global icon sizes\n   - Global hover effects\n\n4. **Block Styles** (`block-styles/index.php`)\n   - Theme.json style inheritance\n   - Custom block style support\n   - Style variation management\n\n#### Theme Integration\n\n**Theme.json Support:**\n- Full integration with WordPress block themes\n- Global Styles inheritance\n- Filter: `stackable_localize_script` adds theme global styles (line 34 in design-library/init.php)\n- Registers: `stackable_global_colors`, `stackable_global_hide_theme_colors`\n- Settings:\n  - `stackable_global_hide_default_colors` - hide default palette\n  - `stackable_global_hide_site_editor_colors` - hide site editor colors\n\n#### Preset Controls\n**Location:** `/src/plugins/global-settings/preset-controls/index.php`\n- UI components for managing global settings\n- Color picker with scheme support\n- Typography controls\n- Spacing presets\n\n---\n\n### 8. ADVANCED CSS FEATURES\n\n#### Responsive Grid System\n\n**Column Width Calculations:**\n- 2 columns: `flex: 1 1 calc(50% - var(--stk-column-gap, 0px)*1/2)`\n- 3 columns: `flex: 1 1 calc(33.33333% - var(--stk-column-gap, 0px)*2/3)`\n- 4 columns: `flex: 1 1 calc(25% - var(--stk-column-gap, 0px)*3/4)`\n- 5-10 columns supported\n- Gap variable adjusts all column widths simultaneously\n\n**Responsive Behavior:**\n- Desktop: Full width calculation\n- Tablet (768px+): Dual column or reduced\n- Mobile (-767px): Single column stacking\n\n#### Special Layout Handling\n\n**Tabs Block (Vertical Mode):**\n- Grid layout: `grid-template-columns: auto 1fr auto`\n- Tab labels on left/right with content in center\n- Responsive breakpoint adjusts to single column on mobile\n\n**Timeline Block:**\n- Grid-based layout with line connectors\n- Dot positioned with CSS variables: `--line-dot-size`, `--line-accent-bg-color`\n- Mobile layout: staggered single column\n- Line positioning: calculated from dot size and content\n\n**Feature Block:**\n- Can switch between horizontal and vertical layouts\n- Responsive: becomes vertical on mobile\n- Image can be left/right via flexbox order\n\n#### Advanced Selectors & Specificity\n\n**Scope Management:**\n- `:where()` pseudo-class for zero specificity increase\n- Example: `:where(.has-text-align-left) .stk-block-divider`\n- Prevents specificity wars with theme CSS\n\n**State-Based CSS:**\n- `.stk--hide-desktop`, `.stk--hide-tablet`, `.stk--hide-mobile`\n- Media query gating for visibility controls\n- Essential blocks: `stk-available-states: [\"enabled\", \"hidden\"]`\n\n---\n\n### 9.
